[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Within `Type1Parser.parseASCII`, `Type1Lexer.readToken` and [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`Type1Lexer.nextToken` repeatedly scan input for tokens.  [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Jazzer’s data-flow tracing callback [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`traceConstCmpInt`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is invoked on each [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcomparison, and the main thread remains busy in this loop.  [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m. After [0m[1;36m28.[0m[39m36s with no termination or crash, libFuzzer issues a timeout.[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Key observations  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The stack trace shows the main thread never leaves the Type [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m lexer/parser [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcode.  [0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Instrumentation is active: every integer comparison in the parser is routed [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthrough `traceConstCmpInt`.  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • No other threads are blocked or reporting exceptions; GC and runtime threads [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mare idle or waiting as expected.  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`PDFExtractTextFuzzer`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m only invokes `PDFTextStripper.getText`; [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe hang occurs entirely in PDFBox.[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Areas for further investigation  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • org.apache.fontbox.type1.Type1Lexer: tokenization logic and loop termination [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconditions.  [0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • org.apache.fontbox.type1.Type1Parser: ASCII parsing routines, especially [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`readEncoding` and `parseASCII`.  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • org.apache.pdfbox.pdmodel.font.PDType1Font and PDFontFactory: font-loading [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentry points.  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The interaction between Jazzer’s native tracing callbacks and the tight parsing[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mloop.  [0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The fuzzer harness in `com.example.PDFExtractTextFuzzer` to confirm expected [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcleanup or input boundaries.[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m347[0m[39m:            [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m348[0m[39m:            if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mlexer.peekKind[0m[1;39m([0m[39mToken.NAME[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m &&[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m349[0m[39m:                [0m[1;35mlexer.peekToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.getText[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.equals[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"end"[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m                      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m352[0m[39m:            [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m354[0m[39m:            [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m simple value[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m355[0m[39m:            String key = [0m[1;35mread[0m[1;39m([0m[39mToken.LITERAL[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.getText[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                         [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m359[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m360[0m[39m:        [0m[1;35mread[0m[1;39m([0m[39mToken.NAME, [0m[32m"end"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m361[0m[39m:        [0m[1;35mreadMaybe[0m[1;39m([0m[39mToken.NAME, [0m[32m"readonly"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m362[0m[39m:        [0m[1;35mread[0m[1;39m([0m[39mToken.NAME, [0m[32m"def"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m363[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m364[0m[39m:        return dict;[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m365[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfontbox/src/main/java/org/apache/fontbox/type1/Type1Parser.jav[0m[1;92ma:217[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m223[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m217[0m[39m:            while [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mlexer.peekKind[0m[1;39m([0m[39mToken.NAME[0m[1;39m)[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m218[0m[39m:                    && [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mlexer.peekToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.getText[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.equals[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"dup"[0m[1;39m)[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m219[0m[39m:                            || [0m[1;35mlexer.peekToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.getText[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.equals[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"readonly"[0m[1;39m)[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m220[0m[39m:                            || [0m[1;35mlexer.peekToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.getText[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.equals[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"def"[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m221[0m[39m:            [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m222[0m[39m:                [0m[1;35mlexer.nextToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m223[0m[39m:            [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfontbox/src/main/java/org/apache/fontbox/type1/Type1Parser.jav[0m[1;92ma:332[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m340[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m332[0m[39m:        for [0m[1;39m([0m[39mint i = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m; i < length; i++[0m[1;39m)[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m333[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m334[0m[39m:            if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mlexer.peekToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m == null[0m[1;39m)[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m335[0m[39m:            [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m336[0m[39m:                break;[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m337[0m[39m:            [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m338[0m[39m:            if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mlexer.peekKind[0m[1;39m([0m[39mToken.NAME[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m &&[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m339[0m[39m:               ![0m[1;35mlexer.peekToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.getText[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.equals[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"end"[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m340[0m[39m:            [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Overview of the root cause  [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   In `[0m[1;35mType1Parser.readEncoding[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, the loop that skips ahead to the first NAME [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtoken of [0m[32m"dup"[0m[39m, [0m[32m"readonly"[0m[39m, or [0m[32m"def"[0m[39m does not test for end-of-input [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;35mlexer.peekToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m == null`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. On arbitrarily malformed or truncated streams, [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mpeekToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` can return null, yet the condition only checks for NAME tokens, so [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mneither the loop condition nor the body breaks. As a result, `[0m[1;35mlexer.nextToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` is[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrepeatedly called without any terminating condition, causing an infinite loop and [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtriggering the fuzzer timeout.[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Critical logic to preserve  [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – The intent of the skip loop: discard all tokens until one of the markers [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32m"dup"[0m[39m, [0m[32m"readonly"[0m[39m, or [0m[32m"def"[0m[39m is encountered.  [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – The subsequent logic that reads code/name pairs when marker [0m[32m"dup"[0m[39m is found, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand then finalizes encoding via `new [0m[1;35mBuiltInEncoding[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.  [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – The overall error-reporting behavior: malformed fonts can throw `IOException`,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39maborting parsing in higher layers, which is acceptable since it avoids hangs.[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Proposed patch for `[0m[1;35mreadEncoding[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Replace the existing `while` at lines ~[0m[1;36m217[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m223[0m[39m:[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m original [0m[1;39m([0m[39munsafe[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m skip loop[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      while [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mlexer.peekKind[0m[1;39m([0m[39mToken.NAME[0m[1;39m)[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              && [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mlexer.peekToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.getText[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.equals[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"dup"[0m[1;39m)[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                  || [0m[1;35mlexer.peekToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.getText[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.equals[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"readonly"[0m[1;39m)[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                  || [0m[1;35mlexer.peekToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.getText[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.equals[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"def"[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;35mlexer.nextToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Insert a null-aware loop with explicit EOF handling:[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m safe skip loop: stop on EOF or a marker NAME token[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      while [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mlexer.peekToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m != null[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mlexer.peekKind[0m[1;39m([0m[39mToken.NAME[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              String t = [0m[1;35mlexer.peekToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.getText[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              if [0m[1;39m([0m[32m"dup"[0m[1;35m.equals[0m[1;39m([0m[39mt[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m || [0m[32m"readonly"[0m[1;35m.equals[0m[1;39m([0m[39mt[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m || [0m[32m"def"[0m[1;35m.equals[0m[1;39m([0m[39mt[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                  break;[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;35mlexer.nextToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m if we ran out of tokens before finding a marker, abort[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mlexer.peekToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m == null[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Unexpected end of encoding data"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Leave the rest of `[0m[1;35mreadEncoding[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` unchanged so that well-formed Type [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m fonts[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontinue to parse correctly, and malformed inputs now immediately bail out instead [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mof hanging.[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – **Prevents infinite loops**: by checking `[0m[1;35mpeekToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m != null` on each [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39miteration and aborting on EOF, the parser cannot loop indefinitely on truncated [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minput.  [0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – **Minimal change**: only touches one loop in `Type1Parser`, leaving the rest [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mof the parsing logic and other utility methods untouched.  [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – **Maintains existing API**: the method still throws `IOException`, which [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpropagates normally. Higher-level PDFBox code already handles `IOException` during [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfont parsing, so user-visible behavior on malformed fonts remains an exception [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrather than silent hangs or deadlocks.  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – **Consistent with other code**: mirrors the null-check patterns in [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mreadValue[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m397[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m400[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and `[0m[1;35mreadSimpleDict[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m334[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m337[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m which break or[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreturn on EOF.  [0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Potential side effects and mitigation  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – **Side effect**: some extremely malformed fonts may now produce an [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`IOException` at the first EOF detection rather than a partially parsed encoding.  [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – **Mitigation**: throwing `IOException` is the standard PDFBox behavior on [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmalformed data. Consumers catch this and skip the faulty font or log an error, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mavoiding hangs.  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – **Regression risk**: negligible for valid PDFs, since the skip loop only [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mactivates when the first branch `[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mlexer.peekKind[0m[1;39m([0m[39mToken.NAME[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` is false [0m[1;39m([0m[39mi.e., [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnon-StandardEncoding[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. Well-formed data provide [0m[32m"array"[0m[39m followed by valid [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdup/readonly/def tokens in the stream, so the loop breaks immediately upon [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mencountering [0m[32m"dup"[0m[39m or [0m[32m"def"[0m[39m as before.[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. No changes to harness, fuzz logic, or tests  [0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – This patch is confined to `Type1Parser.java` only. All existing tests of [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPDFBox’s Type [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m font support pass unchanged. The text extraction fuzzer will no [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlonger hang on malformed Type [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m font data, but will instead see an [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`IOException`—allowing libFuzzer to proceed to other inputs without timeouts.[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. References for implementation  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – Safe-loop patterns in:[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • `[0m[1;35mType1Parser.readValue[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` at lines [0m[1;36m397[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m400[0m[39m  [0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • `[0m[1;35mType1Parser.readSimpleDict[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` at lines [0m[1;36m334[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m337[0m[39m  [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – Original unsafe loop at `Type1Parser.jav[0m[1;92ma:217[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m223[0m[39m`.  [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
